 haalanki NDTV se baatcheet main justise dhingra ne kaha ki unhone aisa isliye kiya, kyonki vah sirf sarkari afasaron se aamane-saamne mulaakaat karnaa chaahate the, or "privet partiyon ko alag se sawaal bhej die gaye the, jinke jawaab unhone daakhil kar die hai
 
 
 " robert wadra ne guuruuvaar ko fasebuk par ek post main likhaa, "sarkaar dwaara lagbhag ek dashak se mujh par lagaae ja rahe jhuthe or aadharahin aarope
 
 
 i will always be used for political gain, i know
 
 
 lekin main hameshaa apana sir ooncha uthaakar chaluungaa
 
 
 " varsh 2011 main sevanivrutt ho chuke justise dhingra ne kaha ki vah apni jaanch ke bare main isse zyaada kuch bhi nahin bataa sakate, jab tak mukhyamantri manoharlal khatter unki report kii samiksha nahin kar lete
 Prime Minister Narendra Modi had promised to get to the bottom of Robert Vadra's allegedly wrongful land deals before the 2014 Lok Sabha elections, and then reiterated his promise while campaigning for the assembly elections in Haryana that same year
 darasal, robert wadra se judaa vivaad gudgaanv ke ek 3
 The plot is based on a deal of 5 acres, which he made 7 in the year 2008
 5 karod rupee main kharida, or kuch hi maheene baad use desh ke sabase bade real estate develper dlef ko 58 karod rupee main bech diya
 Robert Vadra and DLF continue to deny that anything was done wrongly in the deal
 congress, sonia gandhi or robert wadra kii patni priyanka bhi 'phayda pahunchaae jane ke liye kiya gaya sauda' hone kii baat kaa khandan kar chuke hai, or unhone jaanch ko 'rajnatik badale kii karrwai' qaraar diya tha
 BJP says that taking advantage of being in power in the state, the Congress made the desired changes in the rules, which not only sold the land to Robert Vadra at cheap prices, but also approved the commercial use of that land very soon, Due to which, its prices went up a lot till selling
 us zamin saude ko varisht naukarshah ashok khemka ne radd kar diya tha, jinka sirf teen hi din baad tabadalaa kar diya gaya
 Justice Dhingra is probing land deals involving four villages in Gurgaon, including the Robert Vadra deal
 unka kahana he ki jab sonia gandhi kii saas indira gandhi desh kii pradhanmantri thim, unhone sainya vaahanon ko kharid-bikri ke liye feet ghoshit kiye jane ke badale raksha mantralay ke adhikariyon dwaara rishwat lene kii baat khat likhakar unhen bataai thi
 He told NDTV, "the problem with me was that i used to check the quality of every part
 
 
 maine samaj liya tha ki is vibhaag main main katai anfit hum, kyonki adhiktar log kamishan liya karte hai, or main nahin letaa tha
 
 
 i also wrote about this to my department head and Prime Minister Indira Gandhi
 
 
 " Justice Dhingra pointed out that he was 22 at the time, and he also felt good during his early tenure as the Vehicle Inspector of the Ministry of Defense, and had also test-drive a Russian war tank in Ahmednagar, but widespread corruption Because of this, he decided to resign
 unhone bataaya, "hamen har chiz ke liye sangharsh karnaa padataa tha
 
 
 Despite being a laborer, my father understood the value of education, so he completed his matriculation while working, with the help of which he became a storeman in the OD
 
 
 vah chaahate the ki unke chaaron bachche padhein-likhen, or is par vah puraa dhyaan bhi dete the
 
 
 "comments dilli ke ek garib parivaar se aane vaale college vidhyaarthee ke rup main justise dhingra ne khud bhi radio or tivi sudhaarna siikhaa
 Whatever he earned from 30-40 rupees, he used to buy his books and household necessities
 justise dhingra ne apni vakaalat kii degree 1975 main hasil kii or city jaj ke rup main kaam karne se pehle vakil ke rup main bhi kaam kiya
 He later stayed for five years in the Delhi High Court
 sutron ke mutabik, justise dhingra ne jaanch ke liye or mohalat maangate hue mukhyamantri manoharlal khatter ko suchit kiya ki unhen kuch nai jaankariyaan mili hai, jo ki is jameen saude main shaamil sarkari adhikariyon kii pahchaan main madadgaar sabit ho sakati hai
 The retired Justice Dhingra was appointed by the Manoharlal Khattar government of the Bharatiya Janata Party (BJP) nearly a year ago to investigate land deals made by Robert Vadra and other developers during the rule of the Bhupendra Singh Hooda government of Congress
 jaanch ke dauraan is baat par bhi vivaad hue ki dilli hoicourt main jaj rah chuke 67-varshiya justise dhingra ne robert wadra yaa unki real estate company ski lite hospitality ke kisi pratinidhi yaa is saude main kathith gadabadiyon ko ujagar karne vaale varisht afasar ashok khemka ko bhi poochtacha ke liye nahin bulaayaa
 However, speaking to NDTV, Justice Dhingra said that he did so because he only wanted to meet government officials face-to-face, and "separate questions were sent to private parties, to which he has filed answers
" 
 
 " Robert Vadra wrote in a post on Facebook on Thursday, "false and baseless allegations made against me by the government for almost a decade
 
 
 mujhe hameshaa rajnatik phaayde ke liye istemaal kiya jayega, main jaanata hum
 
 
 But i will always raise my head and walk
 
 
 " Justice Dhingra, who retired in 2011, said he could not reveal anything more about his investigation until Chief Minister Manohar Lal Khattar reviewed his report
 pradhanmantri narendra modi ne varsh 2014 ke loksabhaa chunaav se pehle robert wadra ke kathith rup se galat bhoomi saudon kii tah tak pahunchane kaa vaada kiya tha, or phir usee saal haryana main hue vidhansabha chunaav ke liye prachaar ke dauraan bhi unhone apana vaada doharaaya tha
 Actually, the controversy related to Robert Vadra a 3 of Gurgaon
 5 acre ke plot ke saude par aadhaarit he, jise unhone varsh 2008 main 7
 Bought for Rs 5 crore, and a few months later sold it to DLF, the country's largest real estate developer, for Rs 58 crore
 robert wadra or dlef saude main kuch bhi galat tareeke se kiya gaya hone se inkaar karte rahe hai
 The Congress, Sonia Gandhi and Robert Vadra's wife Priyanka have also denied that the deal was to be 'used for profit', and called the investigation a 'political vendetta'
 bijepi kaa kahana he ki rajya main sattashin hone kaa phayda uthaate hue congress ne niyamon main manachaahe badlaav kiye, jinase na sirf robert wadra ko zamin saste daamon par bechi gai, balki us zamin ke commercial istemaal ke liye manjuuri bhi behad jald de di gai, jisaki vajah se bechney tak uski keemten bahut bad gai
 The land deal was canceled by senior bureaucrat Ashok Khemka, who was transferred only three days later
 justise dhingra gudgaanv ke chaar gaanvon se jude zamin saudon kii jaanch kar rahe hai, jinamein robert wadra vaala sauda bhi shaamil he
 He says that when Indira Gandhi, the mother-in-law of Sonia Gandhi, was the Prime Minister of the country, she wrote a letter to the officials of the Ministry of Defense about taking bribe in lieu of declaring military vehicles fit for purchase and sale
 unhone NDTV se kaha, "mere saath dikkat yah thi ki main har hisse kii quality jaancha karata tha
 
 
 i understood that i am unfit in this department, because most people take commissions, and i did not take them
 
 
 maine is bare main apane vibhaag pramukh or pradhanmantri indira gandhi ko bhi likhaa tha
 
 
 " justise dhingra ne bataaya ki us vakt vah 22 varsh ke the, or raksha mantralay ke whical inspector ke rup main shuruaati kaarykaal ke dauraan unhen acha bhi mahasoos hota tha, or unhone ahmednagar main roosi yudhak tanks bhi test-drive kiya tha, lekin vyapak bhrashtachar kii vajah se unhone istipha dene kaa faisla kiya
 He explained, "we had to struggle for everything
 
 
 shramik hone ke baavjood mere pita shiksha kaa mulya samajhate the, so, unhon kaam karte-karte metric kii padhai puri kii, jisaki madad se vah aayudh depo main storeman ban paae
 
 
 He wanted all four of his children to read and write, and he paid full attention to it
 
 
 "tippaniyan As a college student from a poor family in Delhi, Justice Dhingra himself learned to improve radio and TV
 jo bhi 30-40 rupee vah kamaate the, unase vah apni kitaaben or ghar kii zarurat kaa saamaan kharida karte the
